<Text>Lived here for years, and it's a pleasant and quiet family park!

It's a very old place, and a mobile home park, so it's not perfection, but it's also a very unique place to be, with some worthwhile skylines thanks to the open views in the east, and the view between the mountains in the west.

The place is well kept, management does a great job trying to make sure everyone follows the rules accordingly. All have their own reasoning, so understanding and following park rules is fairly easy.

TLDR: Nice place, windy, clean, well managed, pretty skies!< /Text><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMtRsFx65QE7FMf2aI64S3ChepFVTn7vd9wznwa=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNp0DFZnYFTF-mw_czqRuhYL0itR7jz06N5S5tw=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pics>< Resp>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
Clean place and very attentive management. Management is very upfront of park rule enforcement prior to any agreements being signed. Management explains the most common enforced rules, no street parking, no visitors anywhere in the park without residents, children under 10 years have to be under parental supervision,  speed limit must be respected by Residents and visitors, do not alter anything in the unit exterior without prior written approval, ect. Simple stuff. We have lived here 18 years and we seen the place being cleaned up more and more. People that have made negative reviews are mostly people that do not live in the park that feel "entitled" to do as they please, where they do not live. People get emotional and post against management that they do not know. Management does actually enforce park rules and regulations. "Some Resident's" cross the line doing what they aren't suppose to, then they turn around and point the finger at management for doing their job. Management does question people they do not know walking through the park that do not live in the park, there are many no soliciting and no loitering signs through out the park, including signs that warn visitors to go to the space they are visiting, the Park Rules are clear, Residents have to be in company of visitors walking through the park. Then they get on here and make a bad review against management for what they did wrong. They dramatically exaggerate and put it into a bad review. Parents that let their children between ages of 4 years and 9 years old she calls their attention, they do not like it, but, it's their responsibility to keep after their children to make sure they aren't playing on the streets, between the units where the utilities are or being hit by passing cars. That's what those people making negative reviews do not mention. These reviews do not leave room to question those placing these negative reviews. Management is on top of management in the park, the place is well maintained. Quite, secure and a good place to raise a family!!</text>

Sadly this park has a horrible early history. My family has lived here around 11 years now and I can tell you this is a family park. < Review>
Foodies suggest  that if you are within 5 hours of a foodie place you should divert. Follow this advice (generally)...if you are within 509 miles of this place, GO! If you have sworn off hot dogs too bad for you, you are making a huge mistake. Their buns by themselves are worth a three hour detour nevermind their dogs. Buns are sweet and tasty, hot dogs snap in that way that only NYC street dogs do. Get the dog with everything and prepare yourself for a heavenly meal. Again, if you think hot dogs can't be elevated to a gourmand level it's ok by me. The rest of us can only benefit by your conceit.</Review>

< Text>
Restaurant looks nice.
This is not the typical Hawaiian / Orange County style poke place.
I was tempted to give this place three stars however the portions are smaller than average, and you're not allowed to customize the bowl as you go.
I've been to a few other poke places like this and was aware of the style however my friend was not and the staff was not good at explaining the difference.
I feel if they have done a good job of explaining the differences between the style poke and what most people are familiar with I probably would have given them three stars.
If the portion size was up to par with the rest of the Poke places in the area I would have given them 4 stars.
And if I was allowed to customize my bowl as  they made it I might have even given them five stars.<//Text>

< Text>
The Arcane Lab is a great place to find a game of Magic: The Gathering, Vanguard, YugiOh, Pok√®mon and many other card/board games.

The event support is very good Standard (FNM), draft, sealed and commander being the big ones.

The sell mostly cards for standard and a bit of modern cards aswell. Sealed product can vary, but as far as Magic they always have the new sets, commander decks in stocks and sleeves. Aswell as DND stuff, vanguard sealed product and pok√®mon. Binders for commander consists of mostly new stuff with a small variety old or rare* stuff.

I try to buy most of my cards here to support local buisness, but if you're on a tight budget and building budget or trying to find old cards you're probably better off buying it online.

Service: 5/5
Variety: 4/5
Events: 5/5
Price: 3/5</Text>

< Review>
The best gaming shop locally. They run multiple Magic events regularly, EDH and modern for sure, new EDH league starting soon.
As a new player to magic it was really disarming when the shop owner offered to help us with a rules clarification and made it clear we were welcome.
The crowd that visits is really friendly, made new friends the first time we showed up.
Come play and support an extremely-deserving local business.

Thanks for the space you create guys, will definitely be back.</Review>

< review>
When I was looking for a place to stay in Napa I found the Marriot Hotel and Spa. The front of the hotel has this nice waterfall but that‚Äôs it really everything else looked simple. I guess I expected more on the atmosphere and landscape since we were in Napa.

The interior was lovely though. The COVID-19 rules is mandated with masks, hand sanitizer and social distancing. As you walk through the lobby there is a bar at the center and across from was the courtyard which is where the pool is also located. There was a gym and spa but didn‚Äôt get to check it out because on the situation and I didn‚Äôt ask either of the services were available since we only stayed one night.

The rooms were cute. We asked for a queen bed but we got a double bed. As far as cleanliness... everything seems to be in order but it was dusty. All the furniture had dust. So before we could put out stuff down we had to dust the desks, nightstand, and TV area. I would‚Äôve expected it to be spotless considering COVID at least we came prepared.

Note: we can hear the people on each of our sides. The people were very loud.<//review>

< review>
We stayed at this property from 9/24 through 9/28 during our trip to the wine country. The property itself is what I would refer to as a standard Marriott hotel, which is to say good to very good. However, we just did not have much luck on our stay. The first night the air conditioning was not working, the room temperature was 80 degrees and was super uncomfortable. They did fix it and was fine after that but the AC was very noisy, which is common in many hotels in the US. We stayed in room 1143, which happened to be right across the hall from housekeeping, and every day starting at 6AM there was a ton of activity around our room, including an incessant slamming of doors. We brought this to their attention and the slamming, for the most part, stopped but there was still noise every morning. So if anyone is going to stay at this property, stay away from room 1143 and the vicinity. Also note that between rate, taxes and fees, the average nightly cost of this hotel was almost $500 per night.  Trust me and whether it‚Äôs peak season or not, this in no way resembles a $500 per night hotel.  On a positive note, I would say that he staff is courteous and responsive.</review>

<rating>None< /rating>< Review>
This Hotel gets five stars and here's why: This is my first trip the Napa Valley, and I was prepared to "treat" the Boyfriend to a nice resort, with a fabulous pool and spa area, that was in our price range of course. The Napa Valley Marriott fits this bill spot on! After not much research, it's apparent the Napa Valley, and surrounding wine countries are expensive places in which to stay! Finding something I liked that was in our price range, without being TOO crazy, was SLIM pickings. I read the Marriott reviews, and had, like the reviews, a mixed response. From what I researched though, it seemed like a fabulous place that had what we were looking for, and it was SPOT ON! From the moment we arrived, the customer service was simply charming, and so very welcoming. The lobby bar and cozy fireplace area were brimming with happy people sipping wine. The outdoor patio areas with the stylish loungers, fire pits and nightly music was magical. The pool area was perfect after a day out exploring the region, and Marriott's location so close to downtown Napa and many vineyards, was ideal.

This stay was for my bachelorette trip, and I regret to say that this is probably one of the worst Marriott experience for me so far. Here are a few things that were certainly not up to the standard of the Marriott name: 
1. Upon check-in, the receptionist did not recognize my status, and did not mention anything about amenities or lounge access to me. We had to figure all of these out ourselves later (and wasn't able to enjoy the lounge breakfast the first day because we didn't know it existed).

<Name>Dave90212< /Name><time>1546819200000< /time><rating>None< /rating>< Text>
The hotel is close to downtown Napa as well as all of the Napa Wineries.  Ubers and Lyfts were readily available so you don't have to worry about sampling the wines and driving or paying for an expensive car service.  You could get pretty much anywhere in 20 minutes or less during our time there which was "off season".  They also offer bikes during your stay if you would rather bike the wine trail. The room was great and very comfortable, but there wasn't a bath tub (if that is important to you).  I assume it has to do with water conservation in California, but I could be wrong.  The staff is friendly and they have a great spa/work out facility.  In addition, there are table fireplaces out back to lounge around on a cool night with a glass of wine.<//Text>

<user_name>JCH<//user_name><Response>None<//Response><time>1572307200000< /time>< review>
My wife and I planned a vacation in California to celebrate our anniversary, and decided to go with the Napa Valley Marriott Rails and Relaxation package. We booked through the Bonvoy App a month before the event. 
We checked in for our 2-night stay and immediately requested to have more information on the Wine Train package (e.g. where do we get tickets? was there a shuttle to the Wine train? were there upgrade options available? etc.). We were informed by the associate checking us in that we were all set and all we needed to do was show up at the train station and inform them we were with the hotel; If we required more information the concierge would be available the next morning to assist. This turned out to be a complete misinformation.
The next morning, after much back and forth with the concierge, it was finally revealed that additional booking was required, which had not been done. She then called the Wine Train and informed us during the conversation that the lunch package was sold out, and if we wanted to partake in the dinner option for that day we would have to pay full price (over $300 each!). Our only option was to take the tour the next day, which we finally acquiesced to. 
Overall, we felt there was just a serious lack of knowledge regarding the Rails and Relaxation package amongst the staff. Case in point: we later found out that the package we had booked through the hotel was actually the dinner package.
On a positive note, the manager did help quite a bit by offering ways to compensate us for our troubles. Otherwise the rating for this review would definitely have been "Poor".<//review>

<review>Just had a great stay at the Napa Valley Marriott Hotel & Spa. The rooms are spacious, clean and modern (with lots of places to plug in your devices). The front-desk staff are friendly and helpful. The concierge had lots of great ideas for wine tasting, and was able to make last-minute arrangements for a private tasting at a wonderful nearby vineyard (Caldwell) as well as reservations at the top-rated steakhouse in the area (but if you're from NYC, don't bother with the steakhouse--you're sure to be disappointed). The hotel is convenient to a host of Napa wineries and vineyards--both the world-renowned, and the lesser-known.

The morning yoga sessions were the perfect way to work out the kinks from a seven-hour flight. And the spa was convenient, relaxing and reasonably priced (though they could benefit from adding a dry sauna, in addition to the whirlpool and steam room that they offer).

Next time, we'll come in the summer so that we can enjoy the private patio by our room, outdoor yoga and the pool.

My thanks to management and staff for a wonderful vacation!<//review>< pics>

< Text>
At check-in, we were warmly welcomed. It was an anniversary get-away and the woman who checked us in recognized our anniversary. She offered us a bottle of wine and either a cheese plate or a fruit plate. (we chose the cheese plate) We talked about the type of wine we'd like since I am a wine maker. The check-in was a pleasant experience, however, neither the wine nor the cheese ever made it to our room.
The room was nicely decorated however there was no privacy. Cars parked immediately outside the window caused us to keep the blinds closed all of the time. A very "motel" experience.
On the second night, we decided to eat at the hotel's dining room. No one came to our table until I went up to the bar to ask if they were still serving dinner. Being told they were, someone finally came by. The couple at the table next to us had to cancel their order because it took too long to arrive. The waiter told us that there was a $20 corkage fee on the wine I brought and asked if it was ok. I told him no. There was a magazine in our room that listed the corkage fee at this restaurant as $0, and we had an appetizer the day before with no fee. He said he would check with the manager. He never came back.
Lastly, I was awoken in the middle of the night by the sound of water dripping. It was actually coming out of the ceiling in the bath room. Reporting it to the front desk got us relocated to another room. We were offered mimosas and breakfast for our trouble. Never happened.
My experience was not what I expect from a Marriott. Very disappointed.<//Text>

<Review>Overall, another good stay at Marriott. I was in town for work and didn't take advantage of any of the wine related events or opportunities, although they did have that available daily.

Check-in was easy and thank you to Rob for the extra consideration for the gold level membership. It's unusual to receive something without specifically asking for it and that was a nice start to the stay. That said, I had to park on the opposite side of the hotel just to find parking. There was a convention of some sort going on so parking was somewhat competitive at times.

I stayed in an ADA room so the pictures posted may vary from what you see. The far glass doors open onto a small patio area surrounded by foliage instead of a fence, which was different but nice. I saw other reviews mentioning dated decor or condition but I didn't have any complaints for my room. The only issue I had was with what I think was an educator's convention who had some rowdy participants.

The concierge lounge was ok, nothing amazing. They have fairly low volume through there so manage your expectations accordingly. Some of the evening appetizers were delicious though. I had dinner at the restaurant one night and also visited the coffee bar once. Both were good but nothing amazing.

Overall, this was another solidly good stay. My only complaint was with the convention goers and there's not much the property can do about that.<//Review><userid>116638948986269775718<//userid><Rating>4<//Rating><gmapID>0x80850720b5ae9e1f:0xe90d4170a8689308< /gmapID><Name>Jordan Elder</Name><Pics>None</Pics><date>1542918314306<//date></record>

< text>
Napa Marriott is set on a busy street but once inside you know you are in a Marriott resort. There is plenty of convenient parking, the staff is outstanding as are the amenities. Centrally located in Napa with a concierge who can help you enjoy the areas many wineries, it is an excellent place which I plan to continue to use as a base when visiting Napa. Do not overlook the the complementary bike usage. High end cross over bikes provided with bike bags, locks, and helmets. There are outstanding places to ride once you travel a few short miles away from the hotel's busy street. The restaurant is also excellent although the options are fairly standard. My second stay and still one of my two favorite Marriott's.</text>

< Review>
This hotel is definitely nice but wasn't legendary.  The hotel is a spread-out two-story affair located about two miles from downtown Napa.  The location is convenient to downtown Napa (and is definitely the most convenient Marriott brand if you want to do anything in Napa Valley) but it isn't stellar.  It's right on the highway and the setting definitely doesn't scream "spa retreat" to me.  You'll also need a car to get into Napa and it definitely would have been nice to have a location downtown instead of on the outskirts of town.  Location notwithstanding, it seemed otherwise really nice - great staff, good food, awesome pool, etc.< /Review>

<date>1495670400000</date><Rate>None< /Rate>< review>
This hotel is definitely nice but wasn't legendary.  The hotel is a spread-out two-story affair located about two miles from downtown Napa.  The location is convenient to downtown Napa (and is definitely the most convenient Marriott brand if you want to do anything in Napa Valley) but it isn't stellar.  It's right on the highway and the setting definitely doesn't scream "spa retreat" to me.  You'll also need a car to get into Napa and it definitely would have been nice to have a location downtown instead of on the outskirts of town.  Location notwithstanding, it seemed otherwise really nice - great staff, good food, awesome pool, etc.</review>

We spent the weekend here while we toured the surrounding Napa wineries and restaurants. The hotel's design with an interior garden and pool area was really pleasant - our ground floor room had sliding doors leading to a patio with comfortable chairs that overlooked the beautiful shady garden and pool. You really did not need to leave the hotel to have a lovely relaxing stay - it has everything you need, but the temptations of Napa and its wineries and restaurants did pull us away. The location is perfect.  Very comfortable rooms plus they have internet TV which makes it easy to relax and watch your favorite Netflix show or listen to Pandora.  Loved our stay.< /Review>

Very odd layout, had to walk far to room, you may get luckier than I did. The walls are thin, thin enough to hear a couple next door having intercourse. Hotel itself was clean and offers nice amenities: spa, fitness center, lounge with live music and happy hour. The crowd here is older couples and family. Next time I'll be trying a different place to see if I could get more value for my money.<//Review>

<rating>None< /rating>< text>
I again had the opportunity to stay at the Napa Valley Marriott and Spa. I am a Marriott Rewards Member and as always, was treated as if I were a VIP or dignitary. Although, due to scheduling constraints, I did not have the opportunity to enjoy all the amenities offered by this premier property as in past visits, the experience was once again a superlative experience. 

The staff was most accommodating, everyone greeting me with a smile. Because of my compressed schedule, I did not have time to enjoy the spa this visit. Again, because of time constraints precluding my customary visiting of downtown Napa, I had the opportunity to dine in the VINeleven restaurant and bar. I was most pleasantly surprised by the outstanding food and service. The wine tasting buffet in the evening was befitting the Napa Valley. My meal there was an awesome experience. The food preparation and presentation was excellent. My palate was greeted with piquant savor and the staff's suggested wine pairing was perfect.

<time>1490745600000</time><Rate>None<//Rate><Text>Upon booking, I called the hotel and requested an upgrade seeing as I am a platinum elite member, but more importantly because I was spending my birthday at the hotel. Having spent a few previous birthdays at both Marriott and non-Marriott hotels, I was hoping for *some* kind of special treatment or upgrade and the person who took my call said that they'd be happy to do so and specifically told me that my visit would be memorable.
Upon checking in, I got pretty much the same room I had booked, no upgrade, no special treatment and no mention of any birthday at all. If the person whom I spoke with earlier had indeed made a note about it being my birthday, then the person who checked us in didn't even bother to wish me a happy birthday. On top of that, the heated pool - which my wife had specifically enquired about prior to us booking - wasn't very heated so our kids had a less than stellar stay.
That being said, we didn't make any fuss about it during our stay and figured that next year we'd chose another hotel brand at another location. But upon checking out, I was asked how our stay had been and I told the lady at the front desk the above story - and she then surprised me by telling me that she would reimburse the points I had paid the hotel room with. I was stunned and told her that it had not been my intention to ask for such a thing, when telling her about how we felt about our stay. But she insisted and also took the time to wish me a happy birthday, although belated, and I left the hotel feeling a bit better about the whole thing. Now, a week later those reimbursed points have yet to show up on my account, so I guess that I shouldn't have been so quick to reinvest any confidence in the hotel. The semi-good feeling I had efter the checkout is pretty much gone and this is reflected in my feedback and any reviews posted online regarding my stay. I feel like I have been fooled twice by the hotel - first with regard to any special treatment for my birthday and second with regard to the promise of a points refund. <time>1420934400000<//time><rate>None</rate>< Text>
Normally I stay at the NVMH&S for pleasure, using built up Marriott Rewards points for a nice vacation with family. This time, I was attending a meeting, so I stayed for business. As always, the hotel lobby and grounds are beautiful. The staff was exceptional and went out of their way to make my stay great. Of special note was that my company sent me a 30 page document that required 9 hard copies to be distributed at the meeting. I asked the front desk where there was a FedEx Office location nearby to print them since the hotel does not have a business office. The front desk clerk offered to print all 9 copies for me, double sided and collated, for no cost. That saved me time and money! Excellent customer service.

My only slight disappointment was that I stayed on the side of the hotel where the rooms had not been upgraded yet. The new rooms are great, as I have stayed in them before. The old rooms are very nice and very clean, but once you have stayed in the new rooms, staying in the older rooms is a let down. Hoping the hotel will complete their room upgrades soon.</Text>

< review>
Very nice and pleasant hotel. The rooms seem newly furnished and remodeled. When walking in you don't smell that musty old hotel smell instead you smell new rugs, paint and everything you hope to smell when walking into your hotel room. The site says no complementary breakfast but we found that the room behind the bar area serves free breakfast in the morning. They have a 24 hour gym that's well equipped for a travelers fitness needs and a beautiful pool with fire pit seating nearby. The front desk people are so nice and helpful as well. We definitely recommend this hotel to anyone visiting Napa. It's 20 minutes from so good winery's up north.<//review>

< review>
The property itself was great, the rooms were comfortable and spacious, and the location was also fantastic. Where there is room for improvement is the SERVICE. Considering it was a holiday weekend, the staff seemed VERY unprepared and understaffed.

Example 1 - the hair dryer in the room was broken and I called for a replacement. I had to make 3 calls and waited a total of 45 minutes before a new dryer was finally brought up.

Example 2 - there were very limited lounge chairs in the pool area, both days we went we ended up sitting on the ground near the pool and just waiting for someone to leave, and when that happened, it was like a competition with other guests to get to the chair first.

Example 3 - towels. Completely out of towels (both days at the pool) and we had to wait over an hour for towels to be restocked.

Example 4 - Breakfast. We sat outside for nearly 25 minutes and asked multiple times for someone to come take our order. Or even bring menus and place settings. It seemed like there was ONE person managing all the tables outside and in the pool area, which is obsurd!!

Again considering it was a holiday weekend and the property was almost fully booked, you would think you would have ample staff and coverage to provide quality service for the extremely costly price we paid.<//review>

<Date>1411862400000<//Date><rate>None< /rate>< text>
The accommodations were very nice. All of the amenities we needed were there and the bed was very comfortable. The internet functioned well in our room. So, what went wrong? We arrived at 3:00pm and our room wasn't ready. We were told we'd have one in an hour at most. We waited in the lobby a full hour, and had to go back to the desk to finally get into a room (not the one we were supposed to have) with barely enough time to make it to the rehearsal dinner. Water leaked into our bathroom from the bathroom above, and although the problem was fixed, our bathroom floor remained covered in water later that day. Housekeeping cleaned it up well and supplied us with all new towels to replace the ones we had to use to mop up the water. Breakfast in the restaurant was served very promptly and efficiently by friendly, well-trained servers. The food was excellent and the portions were generous. The price was appropriate for an upscale hotel restaurant. We liked the flavored water in the lobby, but on the second day it ran out in the late afternoon and wasn't refilled. We didn't report that, and maybe it was refilled after we left for the evening. Overall, the hotel and grounds were lovely, but we didn't get much time to enjoy them because we were very busy the entire weekend. Without these problems I probably would give the Marriott a higher rating.</text>

< review>
The staff were pleasant and helpful but parts of the property were lacking.  I took several pictures of the sliding door to balcony, the filthy vents in the room and bathroom, the badly repaired tile in the shower, etc.  The bed also did not seem as good as other Marriott properties (Ritz Carlton & Marriott) we have stayed at in Guangzhou/Shanghai, China, Hawaii, St. Thomas and dozens of other Marriott properties around the US.  I never do surveys or reviews but this property was worth the time as it needs some tender loving care in areas.  Water pressure adjusted drastically down to a trickle at times while taking showers and engineering "SUPPOSEDLY FIXED" it.  We kept having the issue off and on and just gave up asking after two times.  They also cleaned the room late (after 4) the first two days.  We had to call and ask what was going on.  They did remedy it and give us some points for the delay, but I would rather not have to deal with it.</review>

<response>None< /response><rate>None</rate><Text>We were in town for Memorial Day/Bottle Rock weekend. Hotel was busier than normal but we expected that.  They were just completing their recent renovation/enhancement.  The look and aesthetic is nice but the details are lacking.  Bed was very hard and uncomfortable. I was convinced the spa chose this to encourage more business maybe?  

Rooms are noisy. Large gap under door let's in all outside hallway noise and when you have the pleasure of getting the room across from the ice machine by the elevator near the exit door overlooking the parking lot that means a lot of noise and foot traffic.  (I suppose someone has to get that room so why not an Elite member right?).  Share with door between rooms has a similar issue so you get to hear all their activity as well (shower, hairdryer, late night fun, etc).  Between that and the bed it is difficult to get a decent nights rest.  

Parking was difficult with the increased weekend traffic and parking lot still being taken up by renovation related trailers, equipment, etc it was less than ideal.  It is a stretch to have the Marriott flag on this property.  Was looking forward to a great stay in a newly renovated property. Unfortunately we got a mediocre stay in a renovation that did not cover all the bases.  Would not recommend at the the Napa prices they charge. Feels more like an Airport hotel than a luxury Napa Spa Resort.< /Text></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
Great place to stay in Napa. Has amble lot of parking, rooms are really well kept and new. Has a good bar -- and a decent size conference room for team offsites.

Located only 3 mi away from Napa downtown makes it an ideal place for a short weekend stay. Has a nice outdoor sitting area by the pool, serves starbucks coffee on demand.

Housekeeping services could be slow, especially if a large group is staying on the days you visit. But overall a good experience for the price they charge. I would encourage you to look for rooms on second and third levels vs the first level -- especially if you like your privacy. The gym is good, but the pool is strictly okay.</Review>

<Text>Was a bit hesitant with all the negative reviews but glad I took a chance. Overall the hotel was clean and staff was friendly. During our time here there was also a convention going on so there was quite a bit of traffic and congestion.

The check in process was a bit painful as they had a live band playing about 30 feet away. Once pass the check in process, we had a bit of trouble finding a space as the parking lot was filled. Overall the room was clean and didn't notice anything dirty. The refrigerator (even though it's behind a door) was grumbling the whole time and the we had one missing glass. A quick call to the front desk and housekeeping brought another one up to us. One suggestion I would make is don't be cheap on the Kleenex. If it looks like it's almost going to run out, save yourself the hassle and just put another box there as that's what happened; we had to call and ask for another box but staff was friendly and quick to bring another one up.

Room service here was very good. The person who brought up the food was friendly. I asked about the spa next door and he admittedly said he didn't know but will find out. Sure enough he did and came back to our room with the information. The room service breakfast (as expected) is on the pricier side but the food is quite good.

For their so called "Resort fee" you do get quite a few benefits for the $20 you pay. You can go downstairs and get 2 free cups of coffee in the morning (this is in addition to what they have in the room), yoga class, fitness center access, and early morning (8:30 to noon) to the spa and sauna. The spa and sauna is next door and it's a must try. Clothing is optional. You can also use their bicycles (there may be a charge but it's nominal).<//Text>< pics>
None</pics>

<date>1342047421929<//date><rate>4< /rate>< Review>
Location is right off of the freeway in Napa, so the access is convenient.  It is not as huge as it seems, since there are conference rooms and the spa.  The pool is nice and open all the time, and their outdoor patio area is incredible.

Staff wasn't nearly as great.  We booked using priceline and ended up with 2 double beds.  The staff worked hard to convince us that we actually had 2 queens, not doubles.  It was a busy weekend and they were booked solid, but it shows that priceline purchases aren't as prioritized as high as if you book elsewhere.< /Review>

< Text>
Rarely do I write a negative review however, our experience at this particular Marriott was by far the most poorly managed Marriott I have ever stayed in.

1)  Concierge: Friday, 9/20/13 - Guests directed to see a concierge, yet no concierge available (4pm in the afternoon) after 25 minutes waiting & a long line of guests waiting, we went to the front desk & they finally sent someone over.

2) Housekeeping:  Friday, 9/20/13 - A guest of the hotel spilled red wine in the middle of the side entrance door where we entered the hotel.  24 hours later the red wine was still there, nobody had cleaned it up.

3) Housekeeping: Saturday, 9/21/13 -  Departed our room early in the morning, came back at 3pm to get ready for a dinner event and the room still hadn't been cleaned.

4)  Housekeeping / Front Desk:  Sunday 9/22/13 - at 6:55AM Housekeeping comes into our room...yes, folks, 6:55AM !!   We called front desk to ask why the intrusion and they responded that someone on staff had errored in checking us out of the room.  So much for early morning romance.

Don't waste paying top dollar Money/Points staying here....was not at all reflective of the Marriott brand I've been accustomed too.< /Text>

<time>1342748647906< /time><Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
In July 2012 my family and 65 of our closest friends and family traveled 3000 miles to the Napa Valley Marriott to celebrate the marriage of my son and new daughter in law.  The actual wedding was held at another venue, but the Marriott was our home base for seven days. All of the staff from managers to housekeepers made us feel welcome.  Whether it was getting rental cars, sending faxes, getting wine openers, or meeting all of our guest in the lobby with wine and olives.  If I start writing about the food in the restaurant, I will run out of space so I will just say "AMAZING"  We could not have asked for a better experience.  If other Marriotts are half as good as Napa Valley, I wil never stay at any other hotel.

Angela Paxhia<//review>

The shower/tub is very small and very basic. Also the TV would turn off at random times. You have to download an app to run it. <name>Sean< /name><date>1435250188855<//date><rating>2<//rating>< text>
Honestly, I was not impressed.  The hotel staff was extremely friendly and helpful.  But the rooms were average at best, with no amenities at all.  This is NOT a resort hotel.  I wish we would have stayed at one of the places in Yountville instead.  Also, be prepared to be nickel and dimed to death here.  But what put them down to 2 stars with me was the restaurant.  They have decent food, but the service is terrible.  It takes forever to get a server, then forever to get a drink, then forever to get food.  The worst part, don't even try to open a bottle of wine from one the various beautiful vineyards that make this area the place to visit.  The restaurant staff flip out on you, even if you are in the courtyard and not at the restaurant, and then charge $15 dollars simply to sit there.  I have never, ever had to pay a corking fee in a common patio area at a resort before.  Ridiculous, especially for the cost of the place.  Use your money at a real resort instead and be treated the way you should, instead of like they are doing you a favor by staying with them.< /text>
